You can decide at which time of the day to get the reminder.\r\n\r\nNotes and symbols:\r\nYou can write notes on any day, and set symbols indicating pain, illness, extra bleeding etc.\r\nThat way you can keep a diary for your period, or practically anything regarding your period/p-pills.\r\nLive Tiles:\r\nPeriod Control supports live tiles to keep you informed.
